## Domain Knowledge (LLM-generated)
**Domain**: population ecology / population dynamics
**Analysis**: This task models population growth rate dP/dt as a function of population P and time t, falling squarely in population dynamics. The relationship likely involves density-dependent growth terms (logistic, Allee effects) and possibly time-dependent environmental modulation.

**Common formula structures in this domain**:
- Exponential (Malthusian) growth: dP_dt = c0 * P (unlimited growth, no density dependence)
- Logistic growth: dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - c1 * P) (density-dependent growth with carrying capacity)
- Gompertz growth: dP_dt = c0 * P * log(c1 / P) (asymmetric sigmoidal growth)
- Theta-logistic growth: dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - (c1 * P)**c2) (generalized logistic with shape parameter)
- Allee effect (strong): dP_dt = c0 * P * (P * c1 - 1) * (1 - c2 * P) (growth with minimum viable population)
- Logistic with harvesting: dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - c1 * P) - c2 * P (density-dependent growth minus removal)
- Logistic with constant harvesting: dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - c1 * P) - c2 (growth minus constant yield)
- Beverton-Holt continuous: dP_dt = c0 * P / (1 + c1 * P) (saturating per-capita growth)
- Seasonally modulated logistic: dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - c1 * P) * (1 + c2 * sin(c3 * t)) (periodic environmental variation)
- Time-varying carrying capacity: dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - c1 * P * exp(c2 * t)) (shifting carrying capacity)
- Richards growth model: dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - (c1 * P)**c2) * c3 (flexible asymmetric growth curve)
- Polynomial density dependence: dP_dt = c0 * P + c1 * P**2 + c2 * P**3 (general cubic density dependence)
- Von Bertalanffy-type: dP_dt = c0 * P**c1 - c2 * P (anabolism-catabolism balance)
- Delayed density effect proxy: dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - c1 * P) + c2 * t * P (time as proxy for lagged effects)

**Formula structure heuristic features**:
- Oscillation damping envelope → Exponential decay envelope f(x)*exp(-c*Abs(x)) for symmetric damped oscillation, Gaussian envelope f(x)*exp(-c*x**2) for localized wave packets
- Saturation/clipping effects → Rational fraction x/(1+x), tanh; for variables with alternating positive/negative in oscillatory systems, selectively apply Abs
- Growth/decay → Exponential growth exp(c*t), Logistic 1/(1+exp(-c*x)), power law x**c
- Threshold/activation behavior → Max(x-c, 0), piecewise functions
- Coupling/cross effects → Product terms between variables x*y, power-law coupling x**c1 * y**c2
- Density-dependent negative feedback → quadratic term -c*P^2 or rational form P/(1+c*P) representing intraspecific competition
- Allee effects (positive density dependence at low P) → cubic structure P*(P-c1)*(c2-P) with two interior equilibria
- Carrying capacity modulation → multiplicative factor (1 - P/K) ensuring dP/dt=0 at equilibrium
- Seasonal or periodic forcing → multiplicative sinusoidal term sin(c*t) or cos(c*t) modulating growth rate
- Per-capita growth rate declining with P → dP_dt/P is a decreasing function of P, suggesting ratio dP_dt = P*f(P) structure
- Multiple stable equilibria → polynomial in P with odd degree ≥ 3, indicating bistability or regime shifts
- Harvesting or mortality sinks → additive negative constant or negative linear term independent of growth
- Dormancy or lag phase → explicit time dependence such as (1 - exp(-c*t)) multiplying growth terms
- Compensatory vs depensatory dynamics → sign of d²(dP_dt)/dP² near zero distinguishes concave vs convex per-capita growth

I need to analyze the Ground Truth (GT) expression and determine if any candidate can match it.

**GT expression:**
```
0.845*(−1 + P/5.115)*(1 − P/34.44)*P + 0.845*(1 − exp(−0.0969*P))*P
```

Let me expand the GT:

First term: `0.845*(P/5.115 − 1)*(1 − P/34.44)*P`
= `0.845*(P/5.115 − P²/(5.115*34.44) − 1 + P/34.44)*P`
= `0.845*(P²/5.115 − P³/(5.115*34.44) − P + P²/34.44)*`

Let me be more careful:
`(P/5.115 − 1)*(1 − P/34.44) = P/5.115 − P²/(5.115*34.44) − 1 + P/34.44`

Multiply by P:
`P²/5.115 − P³/(5.115*34.44) − P + P²/34.44`

Multiply by 0.845:
`0.845*P²/5.115 − 0.845*P³/176.14 − 0.845*P + 0.845*P²/34.44`

Second term: `0.845*(1 − exp(−0.0969*P))*P = 0.845*P − 0.845*P*exp(−0.0969*P)`

Combining: The `−0.845*P` and `+0.845*P` cancel!

GT = `0.845*P²*(1/5.115 + 1/34.44) − 0.845*P³/176.14 − 0.845*P*exp(−0.0969*P)`

So GT = `c₁*P³ + c₂*P² − c₃*P*exp(−c₄*P)` where all constants are specific values.

The key structural components are: **P³, P², and P*exp(c*P)** terms (no t-dependence!).

Now I need a candidate with: `a*P³ + b*P² + d*P*exp(e*P)` (no t-dependence).

This has `P³ + P² + P + exp(P*c)`. But GT has `P*exp(P*c)`, not `exp(P*c)`. Also GT has no constant P term (it cancelled). Close but the exp term is `c4*exp(P*c5)` not `c4*P*exp(P*c5)`.

Has `exp(P*c7)` not `P*exp(P*c7)`.

GT Equivalence Verification (BPG3)
============================================================
GT: c0*(-c1 + P/c2)*(c3 - P/c4)*P + c5*(c6 - exp(-c7*P))*P
Candidates evaluated: 175
Matched candidate IDs: []
Matched candidates: []

I need to analyze the Ground Truth (GT) expression and determine which candidates can match it.

## GT Analysis

The GT is:
```
0.845*(P/5.115 - 1)*(1 - P/34.44)*P + 0.845*(1 - exp(-0.0969*P))*P
```

Let me expand this. First term:
```
0.845*(P/5.115 - 1)*(1 - P/34.44)*P
```

Let me denote a = 1/5.115 ≈ 0.1955, b = 1/34.44 ≈ 0.02904.

First term = 0.845*(aP - 1)*(1 - bP)*P = 0.845*P*(aP - 1 - abP² + bP)
= 0.845*P*(-abP² + (a+b)P - 1)
= 0.845*(-abP³ + (a+b)P² - P)

Second term:
```
0.845*(1 - exp(-0.0969*P))*P = 0.845*P - 0.845*P*exp(-0.0969*P)
```

So GT = 0.845*(-abP³ + (a+b)P² - P) + 0.845*P - 0.845*P*exp(-0.0969*P)
= -0.845*ab*P³ + 0.845*(a+b)*P² - 0.845*P + 0.845*P - 0.845*P*exp(-0.0969*P)
= -0.845*ab*P³ + 0.845*(a+b)*P² - 0.845*P*exp(-0.0969*P)

So GT = α*P³ + β*P² + γ*P*exp(-δ*P)

where α = -0.845*ab, β = 0.845*(a+b), γ = -0.845, δ = 0.0969.

**Key basis functions in GT: P³, P², P·exp(-δP)**

The GT has NO dependence on t. So any candidate with t-dependence that cannot be zeroed out is a NO MATCH.

The critical non-polynomial term is **P·exp(-δP)**. This cannot be represented by:
- log terms
- sin/cos terms
- rational functions P/(P·c + 1)
- power terms P^c

Let me check which candidates have the right structure. I need P³, P², and P·exp(cP) terms, with no t-dependence (or t-terms that can be zeroed).

Let me systematically go through candidates, focusing on the non-polynomial part.

**Candidates with P·exp(c·P) or exp(c·P) terms that could give P·exp(-δP):**

Looking for exp(c*P) terms...

- Candidate 54: c4*exp(P*c5) — this is exp(cP), not P*exp(cP). Missing the P factor.
- Candidate 60: c4*exp(P*c5) — same issue, but has P²c0 + P(c1+c2) + c3 + c4*exp(Pc5). The c3 constant and missing P*exp term make this not work.
- Candidate 63: c4*log(c5*exp(P*c6) + 1) — this is a softplus, not exp.
- Candidate 79: P³c0 + P²c1 + P²c2 + Pc3 + c4*exp(Pc5) — has exp(Pc5) but not P*exp(Pc5).
- Candidate 43: same as 79 but with P/(Pc+1) term added.

Wait, let me reconsider. The GT has P*exp(-δP). Can any candidate produce this?

Actually, none of the candidates seem to have a P*exp(c*P) term explicitly. Let me look more carefully...

The GT's functional form requires:
1. P³ term
2. P² term  
3. P·exp(c·P) term

No candidate has P·exp(c·P) as a basis function. The closest are candidates with exp(c·P) (without the P multiplier) or candidates with completely different non-polynomial terms.

Since P·exp(c·P) cannot be exactly represented by any of the basis functions available in the candidates (log, sin, rational, power law, plain exp), **none of the candidates can match the GT**.
